         <div class="details-section description simple contains-text-link">
          <div class="details-section-contents show-more-container" data-show-height="144" data-show-use-buffer="true">
           <h1 aria-label=" Description ">
           </h1>
           <div class="show-more-content text-body" itemprop="description">
            <div class="id-app-orig-desc">
             This is a Virtual Reality game. Nighttime Terror works only with the Google Coardboard headset or similar devices.
             <p>
              --------------------
             </p>
             <p>
              KILL THEM BEFORE THEY KILL YOU!
             </p>
             <p>
              Nighttime Terror is a VR top down shooter inside your childhood nightmares. Fight against your scary toys and compete with other players for the high score!
             </p>
             <p>
              This demo contains the first level and two weapon power ups. Buy the full version with 6 unique maps and two additional weapons, the Minigun and the RPG Launcher here:
              <br/>
              https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.vrbits.nighttimeterrorcardboard
             </p>
             <p>
              <br/>
              Nighttime Terror is inspired by a Unity tutorial (
              <a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.google.com/url?q%3Dhttp://unity3d.com/learn/tutorials/projects/survival-shooter%26sa%3DD%26usg%3DAFQjCNHRUqzgZWo-2YFkbKtj9x52IzudKw&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNGiuEkK07ezPGwpgcy1dILyXgoSlw" target="_blank">
               http://unity3d.com/learn/tutorials/projects/survival-shooter
              </a>
              ). All the assets in Nighttime Terror are properly licensed or created solely for this game.
             </p>
             <p>
              <br/>
              --------------------
             </p>
             <p>
              Supports Magnet Trigger and Bluetooth Gamepads!
             </p>
             <p>
              --------------------
             </p>
             <p>
              Also available on Samsung GearVR and Oculus Rift!
             </p>
             <p>
              --------------------
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.google.com/url?q%3Dhttp://www.NighttimeTerror.com%26sa%3DD%26usg%3DAFQjCNHvTcYJ-8H1sMc7mtpioWxIpHP_xg&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNGlyt38TiqoWndsjPQb_D2oYa4gZA" target="_blank">
               http://www.NighttimeTerror.com
              </a>
             </p>
            </div>
            <div class="show-more-end">
            </div>
           </div>

              <div class="review-body">
               <span class="review-title">
               </span>
               This game is great, easily the best game I've played on Google Cardboard. I played using an LG G3 and a USB keyboard using an OTG cable.  It runs really smooth, until later levels where the number of enemies grows and starts to slow things down. The only thing I found odd was the infinite height of the bedroom, I guess this helps with performance not having to draw a ceiling, but I was expecting a kids bedroom ceiling with a projected star field nightlight type thing. I'd love to have options to decrease the graphics quality to improve performance, but otherwise a great game and I can't wait to try more from this developer. Maybe I'll go try the vr island survivor game the poster on the bedroom wall shows.

               <div class="description">
                Welcome to The South Korea Aerial Tour.
                <br/>
                This is a joint project between UK based VRCraftworks (http://www.VRCraftworks.com) and Korean VR Photographic experts TheVR (http://www.TheVR.co.kr).  We hope that you really enjoy this app.  We present a unique collection of Aerial 360 degree work completed by the Korean "TheVR" Photographic Team, highlighting some of the most spectacular parts of South Korea.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Please crank up the volume or use those headphones!
                <br/>
                <br/>
                About the App
                <br/>
                The app is hands free, designed for and works with the Durvios Dive (http://goo.gl/UE5f4Z), the DODOcase Smartphone VR Viewer (http://goo.gl/jZNl6y), Google Cardboard and the Stooksy VR. In fact if you have any Smartphone VR Viewer (Cardboard or Plastic) you will enjoy this experience. Download on wifi. With great thanks to Dive, Unity and Playmaker, and the free sounds from https://www.freesound.org/ and http://www.freesfx.co.uk/
                <br/>
                <br/>
                A very small number of devices do not like the large textures we have to use.  If you do have any problems please contact us before giving us 1 star. We will supply you with your own lite version.

               <a aria-hidden="true" class="card-click-target" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.VRCraftworks.Orbulus" tabindex="-1">
               </a>
               <h2>
                <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.VRCraftworks.Orbulus" title="Orbulus, for Cardboard VR">
                 Orbulus, for Cardboard VR
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="subtitle-container">
                <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=VRCraftworks+Ltd" title="VRCraftworks Ltd">
                 VRCraftworks Ltd
                </a>
                <span class="price-container">
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                 <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.VRCraftworks.Orbulus">
                  <div class="pon" style="display:none">
                   1
                  </div>
                  <button class="price buy id-track-click" data-server-cookie="CAIaIgogEh4KGGNvbS5WUkNyYWZ0d29ya3MuT3JidWx1cxABGAM=" data-uitype="223">
                   <span class="display-price">
                    Free
                   </span>
                  </button>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="description">
                Thank you for looking at our app.  Its hands free, designed for and works with Google Cardboard and other Smartphone VR Viewers. You control just by looking at things in a tour look at the next Orb to travel to it.  Lose yourself in the Oxford Natural History Museum or Melbourne's award winning bar New Gold Mountain.
                <p>
                 <br/>
                 Travel the world, stand on Mars, experience the magic of King Arthurs Glastonbury Tor, get married, visit the Salt Flats, experience New Years Fireworks on Hong Kong Harbour or chill looking at the Northern Lights.  Many more delights await.
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                 Relax, Enjoy, Share and Review.
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                 If you do have any problems please contact us before giving us 1 star. A very small number of devices do not like the large textures we have to use. We will supply you with your own lite version.
                 <br/>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Instructions
                 <br/>
                 1.   Use WiFi
                 <br/>
                 2.   Install
                 <br/>
                 3.   Wait for the data download to complete
                 <br/>
                 4.   Run the app
                 <br/>
                 5.   Crank up the sound or use headphones
                 <br/>
                 6.   Relax you have time to insert your phone into your case
                 <br/>
                 7.   Look at a Photo Sphere to choose
                 <br/>
                 8.   Look down to exit
                 <br/>
                 9.   When in a Photo Sphere you can zoom by moving your ear to your right shoulder
                 <br/>
                 zoom out by moving your ear to your left shoulder
                 <br/>
                 10. Relax and enjoy
                </p>
                <p>
                 This has been specifically optimized for the Google Cardboard, but works really well with the DODOcase Smartphone VR Viewer (http://goo.gl/jZNl6y), the Durvios Dive (http://goo.gl/UE5f4Z) and the Stooksy VR.  If you have any Smartphone VR Viewer (Cardboard or Plastic) you will enjoy this experience.  Crank up the sound or use those headphones!
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                 General Information, thanks and credits
                 <br/>
                 The Photo Sphere community has produced some fantastic pieces of photography and until now have been limited to displaying them on flat screens.  Virtual Reality technologies are changing this.  Orbulus puts you in the center of the composition.  We are presenting many of the best examples of this work from around the world, with the creators permissions, for you to enjoy at your own pace.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Enjoy.
                </p>

               <h2>
                <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.Picselica.PocketDolphins" title="Pocket Dolphins for Cardboard">
                 Pocket Dolphins for Cardboard
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="subtitle-container">
                <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=Llyr+ap+Cenydd" title="Llyr ap Cenydd">
                 Llyr ap Cenydd
                </a>
                <span class="price-container">
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                 <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.Picselica.PocketDolphins">
                  <div class="pon" style="display:none">
                   1
                  </div>
                  <button class="price buy id-track-click" data-server-cookie="CAIaJgokEiIKHGNvbS5QaWNzZWxpY2EuUG9ja2V0RG9scGhpbnMQARgD" data-uitype="200">
                   <span class="display-price">
                    $1.99
                   </span>
                  </button>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="description">
                Pocket Dolphins is a Google Cardboard VR experience that transports you into a vivid underwater world.
                <p>
                 In the app you will meet a pair of friendly dolphins that can perform an endless variety of twists, turns, dives and rolls. If you're lucky they might even come up to you for a nuzzle! You can also use the magnet trigger to drop rings into the environment for the dolphins to play with.
                </p>
                <p>
                 If you like the dolphins please rate the app!
                </p>
                <p>
                 IMPORTANT
                 <br/>
                 --------------------
                </p>
                <p>
                 Pocket Dolphins is a demanding 3D app that requires a modern high-powered smartphone (Snapdragon 600 processor or above). Please don't buy the app if you have a weaker phone, as performance cannot be guaranteed..  It has been thoroughly optimised and tested on Samsung Galaxy S4, S5, Note 4, and HTC One and M8 devices.
                </p>
                <p>
                 TECHNOLOGY
                 <br/>
                 ----------------------
                </p>
                <p>
                 The dolphins are driven by a unique artificial intelligence system which produces completely procedural animation. This aims to generate complex and life-like animation, and also ensures that every visit to Pocket Dolphins will be different!
                </p>
                <p>
                 The dolphins are visiting Google Cardboard from the much larger Ocean Rift app for Samsung Gear VR and Oculus Rift.
                </p>
                <p>
                 WHAT IS GOOGLE CARDBOARD?
                 <br/>
                 ----------------------
                 <br/>
                 Cardboard is a low-cost, easy-to-get virtual reality viewer that transforms a phone into a basic VR headset. Learn more about Google Cardboard at g.co/cardboard.
                </p>
                <p>
                 CONTROLS
                 <br/>
                 ------------------
                </p>
                <p>
                 Pull the magnet to drop a firework ring into the water.
                 <br/>
                 Pulling the magnet wile looking at the title on the floor will cycle through different levels of detail:
                </p>
                <p>
                 1. Environment + Caustics
                 <br/>
                 2. Environment
                 <br/>
                 3. Open Ocean + Caustics
                 <br/>
                 4. Open Ocean
                </p>

               <h2>
                <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=org.aprobert.GalaxyDestroyer" title="Galaxy Destroyer VR">
                 Galaxy Destroyer VR
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="subtitle-container">
                <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=LittleAprilFool" title="LittleAprilFool">
                 LittleAprilFool
                </a>
                <span class="price-container">
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                 <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="org.aprobert.GalaxyDestroyer">
                  <div class="pon" style="display:none">
                   1
                  </div>
                  <button class="price buy id-track-click" data-server-cookie="CAIaJgokEiIKHG9yZy5hcHJvYmVydC5HYWxheHlEZXN0cm95ZXIQARgD" data-uitype="223">
                   <span class="display-price">
                    Free
                   </span>
                  </button>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="description">
                "The universe is the dark forest." (Though this one looks a little bright. ;-)
                <p>
                 Aliens from Galaxy Duo have been attacking the Earth. Yet the game-changing space flagship was just built on the Mars base. Warping to the center of one of the Aliens' military solar systems, you, the captain of this flagship, have to destroy the enemy planets and aircrafts before they kill you!
                </p>
                <p>
                 This Virtual Reality game should be played with a Google Cardboard (any compatible model with a functional magnetic trigger). To pull the trigger means to quickly pull the magnetic button down and release. If there is no trigger on your Cardboard, you can still try to tap the screen instead.
                </p>
                <p>
                 To start the game, turn your head towards the start button (itll change color). Wait for a few seconds, or pull the trigger.
                </p>
                <p>
                 In the game, there are several planets to destroy. Pull the trigger to shoot a rocket at the direction where you are currently looking. Alien aircrafts will appear every now and then. Destroy them first! As long as there is an enemy aircraft hanging around (warning signs will show on the screen), youll constantly get hit and lose life. (More enemy aircrafts will not cause more damage, however.)
                </p>
                <p>
                 In the left-bottom corner of the screen are the energy bar and the life indicator (those circle dots). Firing rockets will consume energy and you will not be able to fire when energy level is too low. The energy will recover automatically. You only have a fixed number of life, which is unfortunately unrecoverable. Try to act quickly!
                </p>
                <p>
                 Take a minute off from your work and do some neck exercise by playing this game. Hope youll enjoy it!
                </p>
                <p>
                 --- This game was created for the Archiact VR Game Jam. Made by team Aprobert with . ---
                </p>

                </span>

                <h2>
                 <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.sideloadvr.market" title="SideloadVR for GearVR">
                  SideloadVR for GearVR
                  <span class="paragraph-end">
                  </span>
                 </a>
                </h2>
                <div class="subtitle-container">
                 <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=Mark+Schramm" title="Mark Schramm">
                  Mark Schramm
                 </a>
                 <span class="price-container">

                  </span>
                  <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.sideloadvr.market">

                   </div>

                    </span>
                   </button>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="description">
                 SideloadVR builds custom GearVR .apks that include the user's signature file. This means that developers can share their ideas without going through Oculus Home and the global signing process.
                 <p>
                  SideloadVR is built on the idea of an open system, where developers can freely share their content with an extended tester user base.
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  If you are a developer and want to be included in SideloadVR, please fill out this form and we will get back to you:
                  <br/>

                <h2>
                 <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.skyworxx.wearremote" title="Wear Remote Beta">
                  Wear Remote Beta
                  <span class="paragraph-end">
                  </span>
                 </a>
                </h2>
                <div class="subtitle-container">
                 <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=Mark+Schramm" title="Mark Schramm">
                  Mark Schramm
                 </a>
                 <span class="price-container">
                  <span class="paragraph-end">
                  </span>
                  <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.skyworxx.wearremote">
                   <div class="pon" style="display:none">
                    1
                   </div>
                   <button class="price buy id-track-click" data-server-cookie="CAIaIQofEh0KF2NvbS5za3l3b3J4eC53ZWFycmVtb3RlEAEYAw==" data-uitype="223">
                    <span class="display-price">
                     Free
                    </span>
                   </button>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="description">
                 Wear Remote transforms your Android Wear watch into a remote for your computer!
                 <br/>
                 Use your watch to control slideshows, music player, etc..
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <br/>
                  ---=== IMPORTANT ===---
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  Make sure you have the phone app and desktop client running. The phone app works as a bridge to your computer and has to be running.
                  <br/>
                  Get the Desktop Client here:
                  <br/>
                  http://www.skyworxx.com/WearRemote
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  ---=== IMPORTANT ===---
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  ---=== BETA RELEASE ===---
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  Wear Remote currently maps the gestures from your watch to the left, right, up and down arrow keys on your keyboard. Future releases of the desktop client will make it possible to set up own keys.
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  ---===BETA RELEASE===---
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  Wear Remote consists of 3 parts:
                  <br/>
                  - "Gesture Remote" provides a swiping area and buttons. It will be automatically installed on your watch.
                  <br/>
                  - "Wear Remote" is the phone app that sends the gestures from the watch to your computer
                  <br/>
                  - "Wear Remote Listener" runs on your computer. It translates the gestures from your watch into keystrokes.
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <br/>
                  Wear Remote currently supports 9 gestures:
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  - Swiping in 4 directions, mapped to arrow keys
                  <br/>
                  - 4 Directional Buttons, mapped to arrow keys
                  <br/>
                  - Double Tapping, mapped to the "Enter"-key
                 </p>

                 </span>

                <div class="description">
                 ------------------
                 <br/>
                 !!!!ACHTUNG!!!
                 <br/>
                 Die HTWDD App wird nicht mehr weiter entwickelt
                 <br/>
                 ------------------
                 <p>
                  Die HTWDD App ist alles was ein Student der HTW Dresden braucht!
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  Mit der HTWDD App hast Du jederzeit den berblick zu welcher Vorlesung Du nun musst, wie lange diese noch dauert, siehst sofort welche Vorlesungen Du im Verlauf des Tages noch hast und natrlich was es heute in der Mensa zu Essen gibt. Wie lang geht das Semester? Wann muss ich meine Bcher zurckgeben? Wo steigt heute Abend die grte Party? Die Antworten zu all diesen fragen und noch vielen anderen sind nur eine App entfernt.
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <br/>
                  Features der HTWDD Version 3:
                  <br/>
                  - aktuelle Nachrichten der HTW
                  <br/>
                  - bersicht ber aktuelle und kommende Vorlesung
                  <br/>
                  - 2 Wochen Stundenplan mit automatischer Synchronisation
                  <br/>
                  - Speiseplan der Mensa Reichenbachstrae
                  <br/>
                  - Belegungsplan
                  <br/>
                  - Career Service
                  <br/>
                  - Mentoren Service der HTW Dresden
                  <br/>
                  - Studienangelegenheiten
                  <br/>
                  - Noten
                  <br/>
                  - Prfungsplan
                  <br/>
                  - Bibliothek
                  <br/>
                  - eXma Amt
                  <br/>
                  - Homescreen Widgets fr Stundenplan und Mensa
                 </p>

                  <br/>
                  Erklrung der bentigten Rechte:
                  <br/>
                  - Internetzugriff: fr alle Funktionen der App
                  <br/>
                  - Standort: fr die Karte (derzeit deaktiviert)
                  <br/>
                  - SD-Karte: zum Zwischenspeichern der Karte auf dem Gert (verkrzt Ladezeiten)
                  <br/>
                  ------------------
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  ------------------
                  <br/>
                  Datenschutz:
                  <br/>
                  Die Nutzerdaten und Passwrter werden nur innerhalb der App und zur Anmeldung an den HTW Webseiten und zur Kommentarfunktion verwendet. Zu keiner Zeit werden persnliche Daten wie Zugangsdaten oder Noten an nicht-HTW Server bertragen.
                  <br/>
                  ------------------
                 </p>
